<script>
    let ccpaElement = document.querySelector('.azure-ccpa');

    try {
        let resolvedTimeZone = Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone;
        let timeZones = ['America/Los_Angeles', 'US/Pacific'];

        if (timeZones.find(zone => resolvedTimeZone === zone)) {
            ccpaElement.classList.remove('hide');
        }
    } catch {
        ccpaElement.classList.remove('hide');
    }
